v1 = from(bucket: "gatling")
|> range(start: v.timeRangeStart, stop: v.timeRangeStop)
|> filter(
fn: (r) =>
r["_field"] == "mean" and
r._value > 700,
)
|> count()

|> keep(columns: ["_value", "simulation"])

v2 = from(bucket: "gatling")
|> range(start: v.timeRangeStart, stop: v.timeRangeStop)
|> filter(
fn: (r) =>
r["_field"] == "mean" and
r._value > 600,
)
|> count()
|> keep(columns: ["_value", "simulation"])

join(tables: {v1: v1, v2: v2}, on: ["simulation"])
|> map(fn: (r) => ({_value: r._value_v1 * r._value_v2}))
|> last()
